  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText15911291050958836034" style="display:none"><b>Skulduggery Pleasant is lost on the other side of a portal, with only some evil gods for company. Can he possibly survive? (Yes, all right, he's already dead. But still.) </b><br /><br />Meet Skulduggery Pleasant: detective, sorcerer, warrior.<br /><br />Oh yes. And dead.<br /><br />Skulduggery Pleasant is gone, sucked into a parallel dimension overrun by the Faceless Ones. If his bones haven’t already been turned to dust, chances are he’s insane, driven out of his mind by the horror of the ancient gods. There is no official, Sanctuary-approved rescue mission. There is no official plan to save him.<br /><br />But Valkyrie's never had much time for plans.<br /><br />The problem is, even if she can get Skulduggery back, there might not be much left for him to return to. There’s a gang of villains bent on destroying the Sanctuary, there are some very powerful people who want Valkyrie dead, and as if all that wasn’t enough it looks very likely that a sorcerer named Darquesse is going to kill the world and everyone on it.<br /><br />Skulduggery is gone. All our hopes rest with Valkyrie. The world’s weight is on her shoulders, and its fate is in her hands.<br /><br />These are dark days indeed.</span>

<div id="review_1168823971" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1168823971" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1168823971?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780007325948" href="/book/show/7261549-dark-days">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=magical-fantasy">magical-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1168823971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer205941089846619940"><b>I CANNOT EVEN RIGHT NOW. WHAT WAS THAT ENDING??!! WHAT WHAT WHAT. </b> I glare at everyone who told me this was a good series. I glare and I cry. <br/><br/>It is freaking brilliant but...but....<br/><br/>I HAVE FEELS, OKAY? AND THEY ARE BEING HURT AND MY BRAIN IS EXPLODING WITH THE BEST PLOT TWIST IN THE UNIVERSE!! AFJSDFKALDS I CANNOT BELIEVE IT. <br/><br/>That last page.<br/><br/>The wicked cliffhanger. <br/><br/><b>Okay, okay, I'll actually review the book. But just know that this has been the bestest so far. I give it 4.5-stars only because I thin</b></span>
  <span id="freeText205941089846619940" style="display:none"><b>I CANNOT EVEN RIGHT NOW. WHAT WAS THAT ENDING??!! WHAT WHAT WHAT. </b> I glare at everyone who told me this was a good series. I glare and I cry. <br /><br />It is freaking brilliant but...but....<br /><br />I HAVE FEELS, OKAY? AND THEY ARE BEING HURT AND MY BRAIN IS EXPLODING WITH THE BEST PLOT TWIST IN THE UNIVERSE!! AFJSDFKALDS I CANNOT BELIEVE IT. <br /><br />That last page.<br /><br />The wicked cliffhanger. <br /><br /><b>Okay, okay, I'll actually review the book. But just know that this has been the bestest so far. I give it 4.5-stars only because I think they're going to get even better and I need <i>somewhere</i> to rate higher.</b> The writing is even better than usual and the action scenes seem tighter and faster. There's a lot more bantering dialogue int his one (as opposed to the last). Of <i>course</i> they rescue Skulduggery from the Faceless Ones sort-of-dimensional-hell. That's kind of obvious...but gosh does he come back a little loopy. Unhinged? Yes. He is just a little darker and more insane. I'm very curious about his family though. What happened to them? Oh and about his face, I wouldn't <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ feel right if he had an actual face and wasn't the skeleton anymore. DON'T DO IT CHINA.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br /><br />The humour is just priceless. I laughed OUT LOUD so much. <br /><br /><b>Valkyrie also has huge character development.</b> She's not without Skulduggery for a long time, but she still seems to grow without him. I like how there is no rescuing of Valkyrie Cain. SHE WILL KICK YOUR BUTT BY HERSELF. It's so admirable. She is one of my favourite protagonists in the world. although I do wonder how she can exist with no sleep. It is a wonder. <br /><br />- <b>Tanith</b> is awesome and omg, there is a torture scene that I just about freaked over where <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ they NAIL TANITH TO A FREAKING CHAIR. I was turning pages so fast. It was awful.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />- I actually forgot who <b>Wreath </b>was, but he's the necromancer. From somewhere for something. Ugh. Apparently he's teaching Valkyrie necromancy, I just can't for the LIFE of me remember his context. Google here I come. <br />- I love <b>Finbar</b>. He is hilarious. And stupid. But hilarious. <br />- Also <b>Fletcher</b> is adorable. I thought he was annoying, but his annoyingness is growing on me. I hope he stays. <br />- <b>Dusk</b> needs to be dead. Well, he's undead. So dead again? Please?<br />- <b>Billy-Ray Sanguine</b> is HILARIOUS. He's such a psycho and a villain and I hate him, but at the same time, he makes me laugh. I appreciate a villain with awesome humour.<br /> - <b>KENSPECKLE. </b>NOOOOOOOOOO.<br />- I'm sorry but not sorry. There is just no warmth in my heart for <b>Thurid Guild</b>. <br />- I love Val's parents. I wish she could be with them more....although, then again, I don't. I love her saving the world. But I'm curious about when her reflection is going to do something darstardly. Also it's so cute how <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she's going to be a big sister!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />As you can see, there's a LOT of characters. I didn't even mention them all. I'm exhausted. I do have a hard time keeping up with everyone. <br /><br /><b>Basically, this is the BEST book so far.</b> It has the bestest plot, the greatest plot twists. There's a lot of murder and mayhem and people die bloodily and it's sad and scary. The stakes are ramping up even HIGHER and...it's still funny. Anyone who can squeeze in dry humour into the mayhem of the world being eaten by monsters and exploded with bombs deserves a huge medal. <br /><br />Also Derek Landy's dedications are hilarious. <br /><br />WHERE IS THE NEXT BOOK? I NEED IT.</span>
  <a data-text-id="205941089846619940" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15072513836180789243">When you need lightweight fantasy craziness with ultra-violence, wit and nemeses who just keep on coming back, book after book, your two best options are Eoin Colfer's Artemis Fowl books and Derek Landy's Skulduggery Pleasant novels. The Fowl has gone off the boil (I haven't bothered with the latest one) so that leaves Landy and the Skeleton Detective as possessors of the field. Except Pleasant is stuck in another dimension with a bunch of Gods that appear to have escaped from a Lovecraft story.</span>
  <span id="freeText15072513836180789243" style="display:none">When you need lightweight fantasy craziness with ultra-violence, wit and nemeses who just keep on coming back, book after book, your two best options are Eoin Colfer's Artemis Fowl books and Derek Landy's Skulduggery Pleasant novels. The Fowl has gone off the boil (I haven't bothered with the latest one) so that leaves Landy and the Skeleton Detective as possessors of the field. Except Pleasant is stuck in another dimension with a bunch of Gods that appear to have escaped from a Lovecraft story. Which means Valkyrie Cain, who is the real protagonist of this series, is on a rescue mission. So...how good is Skulduggery Vol. IV?<br /><br /><b> THIS REVIEW HAS BEEN CURTAILED IN PROTEST AT GOODREADS' CENSORSHIP POLICY</b><br /><br />See the complete review here:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://arbieroo.booklikes.com/post/334936/post">http://arbieroo.booklikes.com/post/33...</a><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10217820624225414798">ANGRY NOTE: How could you end Faceless Ones like that, Derek?! With Skulduggery sucked into the Faceless Ones World?! You've got to be kidding me!?<br/><br/>It's official; this series is awesome.<br/>Halfway through the book, I found myself shouting, "Flaming Fudge-cakes! This book is beyond the awesome level!" At the end of the book, I was wiling, "Oh my god! This is just too good!"<br/><br/>Like always, Derek makes me read 3D writing. Oh yeah; 3D equipped with fantastic HD as well.   <span id="freeText10217820624225414798" style="display:none">ANGRY NOTE: How could you end Faceless Ones like that, Derek?! With Skulduggery sucked into the Faceless Ones World?! You've got to be kidding me!?<br /><br />It's official; this series is awesome.<br />Halfway through the book, I found myself shouting, "Flaming Fudge-cakes! This book is beyond the awesome level!" At the end of the book, I was wiling, "Oh my god! This is just too good!"<br /><br />Like always, Derek makes me read 3D writing. Oh yeah; 3D equipped with fantastic HD as well. The action senses, as usual, are well choreographed and well written. (Well, what do you expect from 3D and HD writing?)<br /><br />I wasn't surprised to find that this book was going to be darker than the other books in the series. Here are my few theories:<br /><br />Theory no. 1: Dark Days. It's in the name. Duh!<br />Theory no. 2: Val's growing up, so are Derek's audience. It's exactly what happened to Harry Potter. And it will happen to most series.<br /><br />I can only imagine what the last book in the series is going to be like...<br /><br />If you were to ask me "Who's your favourite character?" I honestly have to think about it. With Skulduggery is the best skeleton EVER, Valkyrie being a Mini-Ninja, Fletcher being charming/annoying-in-a-cute-way, Tanith being a complete trouble maker (I love that!), Ghastly being such a deer, Billy-Ray being pychalogicly derange, and Scapegrace being stupid.<br />Oh, how I love them all!<br /><br />So far, this is the best SP book yet! </span>

<div id="review_259966108" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/259966108" />
    <a title="Shelby Finger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7395988-shelby-finger"><img alt="Shelby Finger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1326291308p2/7395988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/259966108?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelby Finger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelby Finger" href="/user/show/7395988-shelby-finger">Shelby Finger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780007325948" href="/book/show/7261549-dark-days">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer259966108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11741725075263888173">Firstly, Derek Landy is not only one of my top favorite authors, but the author I aspire to be like. His series (Skulduggery Pleasant, starting with "Scepter of the Ancients")fits into the young adult category. The books aren't easy to find in American stores (he's Irish, and given the lingo he uses, it definitely shines through in his writing), so I reccomend looking for them on amazon.<br/> I RECCOMEND THIS SERIES to all ages, and all readers.<br/><br/> This is the ONLY series of books I've ever read, and la</span>
  <span id="freeText11741725075263888173" style="display:none">Firstly, Derek Landy is not only one of my top favorite authors, but the author I aspire to be like. His series (Skulduggery Pleasant, starting with "Scepter of the Ancients")fits into the young adult category. The books aren't easy to find in American stores (he's Irish, and given the lingo he uses, it definitely shines through in his writing), so I reccomend looking for them on amazon.<br /> I RECCOMEND THIS SERIES to all ages, and all readers.<br /><br /> This is the ONLY series of books I've ever read, and laughed out loud like a lunatic in a room completely by myself while reading.<br /> The stories follow a young girl named Stephanie through her adventures as the sidekick to a skeleton detective, befittingly named Skulduggery in a modernized, grittier version of the Harry Potter world (magic users hiding right under the noses of "normal" people). The plots are creative without being too hard to follow, he's hilarious, his characters are compelling (even the bad guys are hard to dislike), and his action scenes are totally bad ass. Despite the fact that this is technically a "children's book," these are quite possibly the goriest books I've ever read in my life. For a small taste of Derek Landy's genius, I highly advise checking out his blog at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://dereklandy.blogspot.com/">http://dereklandy.blogspot.com/</a>, which is often times just as clever as his series. <br /><br /><br /><br />As for <i>Dark Days</i> in particular, I think this is the one that officially won me over for life-- it's also the one where I realized "Damn, this sh*t is getting real." It's WAY, WAY darker then any of the previous books, and really takes Skulduggery's character in a whole new direction. <br />That's all I'm willing to say!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11741725075263888173" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText3925754203461997756" style="display:none"><blockquote> <b>"Be nice," she muttered as they walked over.<br />"I'm always nice," Skulduggery responded.<br />"Don't point your gun at his head."<br />"Oh," he said. Ah, yeah. Fourth book in the series and still amazing. I love the sarcasm, the magic, the characters... I love it. And you know what? When I first read this series it never crossed my mind because, you know, Valkyrie is just so young in the first books. Too young to be shipped with anyone, really. Plus he's a cynical skeleton. Didn't really see him as the realtionship kinda of... skeleton. BUT I think I'm starting to ship Skulduggery and Valkyrie. Maybe not at this point of the story but she's getting older throughout the series. And i'm just gonna go dig myself a grave because I think this reread changed how I view one of my favorite series <i>ever</i> forever...<br /><blockquote> Skulduggery and Valkyrie were meant for each other. <div id="review_100935969" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/100935969" />
    <a title="Paula  Phillips" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1969584-paula-phillips"><img alt="Paula  Phillips" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574564336p2/1969584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/100935969?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula  Phillips" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula  Phillips" href="/user/show/1969584-paula-phillips">Paula  Phillips</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780007325948" href="/book/show/7261549-dark-days">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer100935969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6887081569204055231">At the end of Faceless Ones , we read as Skulduggery was sucked into the portal to the world of the Faceless Ones . In Dark Days , we read as Valkyrie Cain is on a mission to find Skulduggery's real skull-the one that was stolen by Goblins so that she can save him and return him to the real world. As usual , these novels are anything but safe as a new killer -this time one thats been locked up for 200 years and was framed is out on the loose to seek revenge on those - however he can't do this wi</span>
  <span id="freeText6887081569204055231" style="display:none">At the end of Faceless Ones , we read as Skulduggery was sucked into the portal to the world of the Faceless Ones . In Dark Days , we read as Valkyrie Cain is on a mission to find Skulduggery's real skull-the one that was stolen by Goblins so that she can save him and return him to the real world. As usual , these novels are anything but safe as a new killer -this time one thats been locked up for 200 years and was framed is out on the loose to seek revenge on those - however he can't do this without an army of baddies/killers. In this novel we are introduced to Zombies and Vampires -Good and Bad ones. Can Skulduggery be saved and when he returns , is he ok or damaged ?. Can Valkyrie along with the help of friends new and old save the world from destruction from Scarab and his crowd. We also keep hearing about an evil sorceress who is coming to take over the world Darquesse , when Valkyrie discovers news on who she is and that Darquesse is closer than anyone realises . Its time to decide who Valkyrie is to be and become. Will she take a path of good or when the time arrives will she turn her back and let the evil side takeover. An excellent novel , that Im glad I perservered and picked up as If I hadnt I probably would have continued to think it was about Pirates LOL :). I also read a rumour that their is to be nine books in the series and a movie -lets keep our ears and eyes on the lookout to see if thats true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6887081569204055231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3363099123" />
    <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby"><img alt="Ryan Buckby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528436487p2/32429909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3363099123?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ryan Buckby" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby">Ryan Buckby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3363099123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6592092074094470917"><b> "Until the end."<br/><br/>"Until the end.” </b><br/><br/><br/>I am really impressed with how this book went and it's honestly just become my favourite book in the entire series so far. The writing is at it's best right now at this point of the series and i am really digging the direction that it's taken off to! <br/><br/>Dark Days seems to me it sounds more grown up and i love that we see Valkyrie in a whole new way and i love how mature she has become in these four books of the series. Her own character growth has been on the up an</span>
  <span id="freeText6592092074094470917" style="display:none"><b> "Until the end."<br /><br />"Until the end.” </b><br /><br /><br />I am really impressed with how this book went and it's honestly just become my favourite book in the entire series so far. The writing is at it's best right now at this point of the series and i am really digging the direction that it's taken off to! <br /><br />Dark Days seems to me it sounds more grown up and i love that we see Valkyrie in a whole new way and i love how mature she has become in these four books of the series. Her own character growth has been on the up and up ever since the story began and i love the direction this character is headed and cannot wait to see where she goes next. <br /><br />As i said before in my previous reviews that this book was missing something and for me everything this book has is what the other 3 were missing for me personally. Every single character is at there best right now and that's also down to the side characters as well and i hope this continues in the series. All the character relationships have been built more and added on to in this one and i love where they are all at. <br /><br /><br />I really don't have anything negative to say about this book it was strong from beginning to end and i got through this one real fast. Book 5 has a lot to live up to and i hope that it continues on to have this strong streak because this book has kept my interest in the series alive. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6592092074094470917" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UmKeTbzBUC6oOG46WHuzfzxrBrQiAs/0DQtqKytXMvpoRPefB5+ZRg8T2luvjrmg6jThfOyPQZNWdSya5hTAYA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('erzBTajEXMfmzrs8t5Pu7IIuoeLFktAXwoWVHtxLIcpAmqifE5qVr0HlD11AZuQzVHFGKgsfXnCZ+9OvEQjTUA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer507246413071234942">Derek Landy is an Irish writer and screenwriter. In addition to the bestselling children's/YA series of <i>Skulduggery Pleasant</i> books, a supernatural mystery series starring Skulduggery Pleasant, a skeleton detective, and Valkyrie Cain, a young female magician, he has written two screenplays that have been made into films: the IFTA award winning "Dead Bodies" and the IFTA nominated "Boy Eats Girl". L</span>
  <span id="freeText507246413071234942" style="display:none">Derek Landy is an Irish writer and screenwriter. In addition to the bestselling children's/YA series of <i>Skulduggery Pleasant</i> books, a supernatural mystery series starring Skulduggery Pleasant, a skeleton detective, and Valkyrie Cain, a young female magician, he has written two screenplays that have been made into films: the IFTA award winning "Dead Bodies" and the IFTA nominated "Boy Eats Girl". Landy himself was nominated for an IFTA for Best Script. <br /><br />He doesn’t like to brag about all the awards he’s won, such as the Irish Book of the Decade, or the Red House in the UK, or all the other awards that he humbly displays on his mantelpiece. He is also far too modest to mention things like the first book being a Publisher’s Weekly Best Book of the Year, but would like to extend an invitation to Oprah to pop around one day for tea, in thanks for selecting his book for the Oprah’s Book Club Kids Reading List. <br /><br />Derek plays too many video games, reads too many comics, and watches too many movies. He lives in Ireland with too many cats. Occasionally he talks to real people, but only when he absolutely has to.</span>
